[30;1m131 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m132 | [0m[35mThat is obviously not a proper response -- yet. If the protocol returned a[0m
[30;1m133 | [0m[35mfinished response, the program couldn't do any work in the meantime. Instead,[0m
